      Just hearing the name attracted me, so I gave up questioning the formaldehyde problem and chose to go to the new "service first" store to enjoy it (be prepared to go down the mountain and go to the hotel to be in a daze). However, my expectations were still a bit high, and I rarely give hotel reviews. Here is what I do Check-in experience‚Ä¶
  
      Location 
       
      The hotel is located within five kilometers of Hongcun and Xidi. It is indeed not far away, but don‚Äôt give up hope of taking a taxi (because taxis and Didi here have the right not to accept orders within a short range). If you don‚Äôt have a car, Customers need to consider carefully. It does not matter if they drive by themselves. Thank you to the hotel management for arranging 2 trips to the destination.

      environment

      This is a designer hotel. From every brick and tile to the display space layout in every corner, there is nothing wrong with it. The most praiseworthy thing for me is the doorbell design. It is very exquisite, including green plants. Be sure to take a closer look. , but lacks a unique fragrance that is owned by the hotel, and people who understand themselves understand themselves. This time I requested to be transferred from a tatami room to a courtyard room. The courtyard room is indeed not as comfortable as the balcony room. It is more depressing. It may be because of the high walls. The floor in the room is empty because of the added floor heating. The toilet is so-called fully automatic. , in fact, it‚Äôs just a toilet seat. It really doesn‚Äôt match the bathroom as a whole. I asked for the bathtub to be disinfected, but no one responded at all.
      
      Serve

      This is also the soul of the hotel. I believe that customers who come to your place want warm service, unless one day you have special projects to balance each other; I can guarantee that there is no butler-style service. What I see when I enter the hotel is that every With a cold face, the restaurant service staff must not be too demanding, otherwise they will yell at you in dialect. name:S‚Äçt‚Äçe‚Äçp‚Äçh‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçc‚Äça‚Äço
info:Duplex Family Friendly Suite
info:Stayed in August 2023
info:Family
info:19 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted August 7, 2023
msg:Let me summarize first. The hotel has many advantages, but some experiences made me collapse.

advantage:
The design that combines modernity and Huizhou granary is very eye-catching. From the lobby to the rooms to the restaurant, everything is full of design. The rooftop infinity swimming pool is very beautiful. You can overlook the surrounding Huizhou villages while swimming, which is very pleasant. The waiters are enthusiastic and courteous, and the garage security men are particularly enthusiastic. The room is large and has a complete range of toiletries, including children's supplies. You can take a bath. The location is okay, 5-10 minutes drive from Hongcun Lucun and 20 minutes drive to Xidi.

Let's talk about the disadvantages (I personally find it hard to bear):
The air conditioner outlet faces the bed on the second floor. If the air conditioner is turned up, cold air will blow directly onto the bed, making it impossible to sleep on the second floor. If the air conditioner is turned down, the first floor will be extremely hot. It would be difficult for a family of two adults and two children to sleep well in a loft room. Then there is the obvious low-frequency resonance caused by the outdoor unit of the air conditioner. However, this depends on the individual situation. I can't stand it, so I didn't sleep all night (this was the first time I had insomnia while staying in a hotel). The infinity pool is very beautiful, but it is not hygienic. 1. Much more thought was put into the exterior decoration of this hotel than the interior. The interior is much shabby and not worth the price;
2. The water in the so-called infinity swimming pool is changed every time I don‚Äôt know how often. The customer service said that cleaning powder has been sprinkled. The actual water in the pool is very turbid. However, there are no guests in it, so it is of no use.
3. The most important thing is that the location of this hotel is not good. It is difficult to take a taxi. If you want to catch a car or a flight, be careful! The hotel doesn't offer free drop-off. They say they can contact a taxi, but it takes a long time and is more expensive than taking a taxi yourself? ? ! !
In summary, all things considered, this hotel is only worth about 300 per day.
